# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 07:45:30.746846

### Base Program

```py
def numberOfSubarraysWithZeroes(nums):
    count = 0
    zero_count = 0

    for num in nums:
        if num == 0:
            zero_count += 1
            count += zero_count
        else:
            zero_count = 0

    return count
```

## Test Case 1

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def numberOfSubarraysWithZeroes(nums):
    count = 0
    zero_count = 0

    for num in nums:
        if num == 0:
            zero_count += 1
            count += zero_count
        else:
            zero_count = 0

    return count



```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def numberOfSubarraysWithZeroes(nums):
    count = 0
    zero_count = 0

    for num in nums:
        if num == 0:
            zero_count += 1
            count += zero_count
        else:
            zero_count = 0

    return count



```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def numberOfSubarraysWithZeroes(nums):
    count = 0
    zero_count = 0

    for num in nums:
        if num == 0:
            zero_count += 1
            count += zero_count
        else:
            zero_count = 0

    return count



```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def numberOfSubarraysWithZeroes(nums):
    count = 0
    zero_count = 0

    for num in nums:
        if num == 0:
            zero_count += 1
            count += zero_count
        else:
            zero_count = 0

    return count



```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def numberOfSubarraysWithZeroes(nums):
    count = 0
    zero_count = 0

    for num in nums:
        if num == 0:
            zero_count += 1
            count += zero_count
        else:
            zero_count = 0

    return count



```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def numberOfSubarraysWithZeroes(nums):
    count = 0
    zero_count = 0

    for num in nums:
        if num == 0:
            zero_count += 1
            count += zero_count
        else:
            zero_count = 0

    return count



```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def numberOfSubarraysWithZeroes(nums):
    count = 0
    zero_count = 0

    for num in nums:
        if num == 0:
            zero_count += 1
            count += zero_count
        else:
            zero_count = 0

    return count



```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def numberOfSubarraysWithZeroes(nums):
    count = 0
    zero_count = 0

    for num in nums:
        if num == 0:
            zero_count += 1
            count += zero_count
        else:
            zero_count = 0

    return count



```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def numberOfSubarraysWithZeroes(nums):
    count = 0
    zero_count = 0

    for num in nums:
        if num == 0:
            zero_count += 1
            count += zero_count
        else:
            zero_count = 0

    return count



```
